                                    6646              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6647              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6648              Ÿ  RECORD PAGE                                                        Ÿ
                                    6649              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6650              Ÿ  THE RECORD GROUP IS A GENERALIZED STRUCTURE AND MAY BE USED        Ÿ
                                    6651              Ÿ  TO HOLD SEVERAL TYPES AND FORMATS OF RECORDS.  EACH RECORD         Ÿ
                                    6652              Ÿ  PAGE CONTAINS A SORTED INDEX LIST OF THE RECORDS ON THE PAGE       Ÿ
                                    6653              Ÿ  AND ALSO THE ASSOCIATED RECORDS.  THE INDEXES ARE BINARY           Ÿ
                                    6654              Ÿ  SEACHED AND CONSIST OF THE RECORD NAME AND AN OFFSET POINTER       Ÿ
                                    6655              Ÿ  TO THE RECORD DATA.  THE RECORD DATA IS PLACED AT THE END OF       Ÿ
                                    6656              Ÿ  THE PAGE.  THE RECORD DATA GROWS UP AS MORE RECORDS ARE            Ÿ
                                    6657              Ÿ  ADDED, LIKEWIZE THE RECORD INDEX ENTRIES GROWS DOWN.  IN           Ÿ
                                    6658              Ÿ  ADDITION TO A NAME, EACH RECORD HAS A SET NUMBER ASSOCIATED        Ÿ
                                    6659              Ÿ  WITH IT.  THUS EACH RECORD IS  UNIQUELY SPECIFIED BY A             Ÿ
                                    6660              Ÿ  RECORD GROUP POINTER, A SET NUMBER, AND A NAME.  A SET             Ÿ
                                    6661              Ÿ  NUMBER, AND A NAME TOGETHER WILL BE REFERED TO AS THE RECORD       Ÿ
                                    6662              Ÿ  KEY. (THE INDEX ENTRIES ACTUALLY CONTAIN RECORD KEYS, NOT          Ÿ
                                    6663              Ÿ  JUST THE NAMES.)  RECORD NAMES ARE FIXED LENGTH FOR EACH           Ÿ
                                    6664              Ÿ  RECORD GROUP.  DIG IT !                                            Ÿ
                                    6665              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6666              Ÿ  PAGE USAGE:                                                        Ÿ
                                    6667              Ÿ    PAGE A - PAGE A IS THE PRIMARY PAGE AREA.  ONLY IF TWO           Ÿ
                                    6668              Ÿ             PAGES ARE USED SIMULTANEOUSLY IS PAGE B USED.           Ÿ
                                    6669              Ÿ             PAGE A IS NEVER PFREED.                                 Ÿ
                                    6670              Ÿ    PAGE B - SECONDARY PAGE AREA, USED ONLY WHEN TWO PAGES           Ÿ
                                    6671              Ÿ             ARE NEEDED SIMULTANEOUSLY.  PAGE B MUST BE PFREED       Ÿ
                                    6672              Ÿ             IMMEDIATELY AFTER USE. (PBR SHOULD BE ZERO ON           Ÿ
                                    6673              Ÿ             ENTRY TO ALL ROUTINES!)                                 Ÿ
                                    6674              Ÿ  THESE PAGE USAGE RULES, PROVIDE EFFICIENCY - USUALLY THE PAGE      Ÿ
                                    6675              Ÿ  WE WANT IS ALREADY IN PAGE A.  AND ORDER - THE PAGE WE WANT IN     Ÿ
                                    6676              Ÿ  PAGE A IS NEVER IN PAGE B. (A SITUATION THAT CAUSES A FAILSOFT)    Ÿ
                                    6677              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6678              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                                      ¾þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþ»

                                    6790              *  RECORD INDEX ENTRY EQU'S
                                    6791              *
                                    6792              *  NOTE:
                                    6793              *     A RECORD KEY IS:
                                    6794              *        4 BYTE RECORD SET NUMBER
                                    6795              *        N BYTE RECORD NAME  (N < MXNAMELN)
                                    6796              *
                                    6797              * THE TERMS ARE ARBITRARY BUT WE TRY TO BE CONSISTENT !

                                    6801              MXNTRYLN EQU   MXKEYLN+L'DATAPTR+L'DATALN
                                    6802              MXDATALN EQU   2048                ARBITRARY, MAX ~< PAGESIZE/10

                                   11865              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   11866              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   11867              Ÿ  XCNTRECS  - COUNT A RANGE OF RECORDS                               Ÿ
                                   11868              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   11869              Ÿ  COUNT ALL RECORDS FROM RECORD #1 TO RECORD #2 INCLUSIVE.           Ÿ
                                   11870              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   11871              Ÿ  ON ENTRY:                                                          Ÿ
                                   11872              Ÿ     @R15 - RECORD GROUP INFO BLOCK                                  Ÿ
                                   11873              Ÿ            (CONTAINS SET NUMBER OF FIRST RECORD)                    Ÿ
                                   11874              Ÿ      @R0 - NAME OF FIRST RECORD                                     Ÿ
                                   11875              Ÿ      @R1 - NAME OF SECOND RECORD                                    Ÿ
                                   11876              Ÿ       R2 - SET NUMBER OF SECOND RECORD                              Ÿ
                                   11877              Ÿ            (ZERO IMPLIES SAME AS FIRST)                             Ÿ
                                   11878              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   11879              Ÿ  ON EXIT:                                                           Ÿ
                                   11880              Ÿ       R0 - TOTAL BYTE COUNT (DATA ONLY) OF RECORDS                  Ÿ
                                   11881              Ÿ      R15 - (and CC) NUMBER OF RECORDS                               Ÿ

                                   14446              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14447              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14448              Ÿ  ADDDPAGE - ADD A NEW DATA PAGE                                     Ÿ
                                   14449              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14450              Ÿ  ON ENTRY:                                                          Ÿ
                                   14451              Ÿ     @R15 - RECORD GROUP INFO BLOCK                                  Ÿ
                                   14452              Ÿ            (CONTAINS ROOT PAGE POINTER, SPLIT INFO !)               Ÿ
                                   14453              Ÿ      PAR - PAGE TO SPLIT                                            Ÿ
                                   14454              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14455              Ÿ  ON EXIT:                                                           Ÿ
                                   14456              Ÿ       **  - THE GIVEN PAGE IS SPLIT AND THE MASTER INDEX UPDATED.   Ÿ
                                   14457              Ÿ             IF A MASTER INDEX DOES NOT EXIST ONE IS CREATED.        Ÿ
                                   14458              Ÿ       PAR - WILL CONTAIN MASTER INDEX, ALL DATA PAGES PFREED        Ÿ
                                   14459              Ÿ       R15 - CC=ZERO,                                                Ÿ
                                   14460              Ÿ             CC=NZ, IF MASTER PAGE FULL !  (VERY HARD TO DO!)        Ÿ
                                   14461              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14462              Ÿ  ORDER OF EVENTS:                                                   Ÿ
                                   14463              Ÿ       WE MAKE A COPY OF @PAR ONTO @PBR, THE WE CALCULATE            Ÿ
                                   14464              Ÿ       THE SPLIT POINT.  AND SET UP 2ND HALF OF SPLIT @PBR.          Ÿ
                                   14465              Ÿ       THEN WE SET UP THE FIRST HALF OF THE SPLIT @PAR.  WE THEN     Ÿ
                                   14466              Ÿ       UPDATE THE MASTER INDEX TO POINT AT THESE NEW PAGES.          Ÿ
                                   14467              Ÿ       SHOULD THERE BE A CRASH,, I HOPE LINKS WILL ALLOW ERROR       Ÿ
                                   14468              Ÿ       FREE RECOVERY !                                               Ÿ
                                   14469              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ

                                   15305              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   15306              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   15307              Ÿ  MKMASTER - MAKE AND INITIALIZE A MASTER INDEX PAGE                 Ÿ
                                   15308              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   15309              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   15310              Ÿ  ON ENTRY:                                                          Ÿ
                                   15311              Ÿ     @R15 - RECORD GROUP INFO BLOCK                                  Ÿ
                                   15312              Ÿ      PAR - CURRENT SINGLE DATA PAGE                                 Ÿ
                                   15313              Ÿ  ON EXIT:                                                           Ÿ
                                   15314              Ÿ       PAR - CURRENT DATA PAGE, RELOCATED, SEE COMMENTS BELOW        Ÿ
                                   15315              Ÿ       R15 - CC=ZERO                                                 Ÿ
                                   15316              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   15317              Ÿ  THIS ROUTINE IS USED TO CREATE A MASTER INDEX PAGE.  IT IS         Ÿ
                                   15318              Ÿ  CALLED WHEN WE SPLIT THE FIRST AND ONLY DATA PAGE INTO             Ÿ
                                   15319              Ÿ  MULTIPLE DATA PAGES, WITH AN INDEX.  IT IS IMPERATIVE THAT         Ÿ
                                   15320              Ÿ  THE DATA PAGE BE COPIED TO A NEW PAGE (THAT WILL LATER BE          Ÿ
                                   15321              Ÿ  SPLIT.)  AND THAT THE INDEX PAGE BE CREATED ON THE CURRENT         Ÿ
                                   15322              Ÿ  PAGE.  WHY, BECAUSE THEN THE RECORD GROUP ROOT PAGE POINTER        Ÿ
                                   15323              Ÿ  STAYS THE SAME, (IE. THE REC GROUP PAGE POINTER POINTS EITHER      Ÿ
                                   15324              Ÿ  TO A MASTER INDEX,, OR A SINGLE UNSPLIT DATA PAGE.)  OH YEAH !     Ÿ
                                   15325              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   15326              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ

                                   18732              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18733              Ÿ  BSINIT - INITIALIZE BINARY SEARCH INFO                             Ÿ
                                   18734              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18735              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18736              Ÿ  ON ENTRY:                                                          Ÿ

                                   18745              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18746              Ÿ  THE BS (BINARY SEARCH) ROUTINES CONSIST OF BSINIT, BSEARCH,        Ÿ
                                   18747              Ÿ  AND BINSERT.  THEY ARE USED TO HANDLE GENERALIZED BINARY           Ÿ
                                   18748              Ÿ  SEARCHING AND INSERTING.                                           Ÿ
                                   18749              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18750              Ÿ  NOTE THAT THE LENGTHS PASSED TO BSINIT MUST BE REASONABLE          Ÿ
                                   18751              Ÿ  NON-ZERO VALUES. DFJL DAFLK DALKJD. THE TOTAL LENGTH MUST          Ÿ
                                   18752              Ÿ  BE LARGE ENOUGH TO HOLD AT LEAST 4 ENTRIES.  IF YOU INTEND         Ÿ
                                   18753              Ÿ  DO INSERTS THE TOTAL LENGTH MUST BE LESS THAN ABOUT 12K AS         Ÿ
                                   18754              Ÿ  THE STACK IS USED FOR A TEMP AREA.                                 Ÿ

 002428 5040 6010            00010 18817                       ST    R4,BSEND
                                   18818
                                   18819                       COMMENT
                                   18820              *  WE CALCULATE THE NUMBER OF SEARCH ITERATIONS,, IN MATH JARGON
                                   18821              *  WE CALCULATE  LOG(TOTAL LEN/ENTRY LEN) IN BASE 2  ROUNDED
                                   18822              *  UP TO THE NEAREST INTEGER. IN SIMPLE TERMS, WE COUNT HOW MANY
                                   18823              *  TIMES WE MUST DOUBLE THE ENTRY LENGTH UNTIL WE REACH THE TOTAL
                                   18824              *  LENGTH,,, THIS GIVES US THE SEARCH COUNT.   SEE BELOW.
 00242C 5810 6000            00000 18825                       L     R1,BSTLEN           R1 - TOTAL LENGTH
 002430 5820 6004            00004 18826                       L     R2,BSELEN           R2 - DOUBLING ENTRY LENGTH

 002440 4133 0001            00001 18846  1                      LA    R3,1(R3)
 002444 47F0 7022            02436 18847                       END
 002448 5030 6014            00014 18852                       ST    R3,BSCNT            SAVE CALCULATED SEARCH COUNT
                                   18853              * WE CALCULATE LOCATION TO START SEARCH,, FORGET THE MATH JARGON.

0                                  18854              * IN SIMPLE TERMS, WE DOUBLE THE ENTRY LENGTH UNTIL WE REACH AT
                                   18855              * LEAST 1/2 THE TOTAL LENGTH.  (THAT IS WE TAKE 1/2 THE LENGTH
                                   18856              * THAT WE CALCULATED ABOVE.)  THINK ABOUT IT.  OR DON'T BOTHER.

 002460 5030 6018            00018 18891  1                      ST    R3,BSSTART
 002464                            18892                       END
                                   18896              * AN EXAMPLE
                                   18897              * IF TOTAL LEN=512 AND ENTRY LEN=64, WE KNOW THAT 2*2*2*2*64=512
                                   18898              * SO THE SEARCH COUNT IS 4. AND THE STARTING SEARCH OFFSET IS 256.
                                   18899              * ANOTHER EXAMPLE
                                   18900              * IF TOTAL LEN=50 AND THE ENTRY IS 7, WE KNOW THAT 2*2*2*7=56
                                   18901              * SO THE SEARCH COUNT IS 3. AND  THE STARTING OFFSET IS 28.

                                   19736              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   19737              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   19738              Ÿ  ABSEARCH - BINARY SEARCH, ALLOWING ABREVIATIONS !                  Ÿ
                                   19739              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   19740              Ÿ  THIS ROUTINE ALLOWS ABREVIATIONS TO MATCH.  SEE DETAILS BELOW.     Ÿ
                                   19741              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   19742              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   19743              Ÿ  ON ENTRY:                                                          Ÿ
                                   19744              Ÿ       R0 - ADDRESS OF BSINFO                                        Ÿ

                                   19752              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   19753              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   19754              Ÿ  THIS ROUTINE IS SIMILAR TO BSEARCH.  THE DIFFERENCE IS THAT        Ÿ
                                   19755              Ÿ  BSEARCH FINDS ONLY EXACT MATCHES, WHEREAS THIS ROUTINE WILL        Ÿ
                                   19756              Ÿ  MATCH IF THE NON-BLANK PORTION OF THE SEARCH KEY MATCHES THE       Ÿ
                                   19757              Ÿ  ALL OR THE FIRST PART OF THE KEYWORD.  A MINIMUM OF 3 CHARS        Ÿ
                                   19758              Ÿ  MUST MATCH.  IF THERE ARE MULTIPLE MATCHES, THEN THE FIRST         Ÿ
                                   19759              Ÿ  MATCHING KEYWORD IN THE LIST WILL BE RETURNED.  USED TO            Ÿ
                                   19760              Ÿ  SEARCH THE SYSTEM VARIABLE/FUNCTION/PROCEDURE TABLE.               Ÿ
                                   19761              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   19762              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
